## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2-extended-rights"></a><span data-ttu-id="2148f-1288">Direitos estendidos do Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2148f-1288">Windows Server 2003 R2 Extended Rights</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2148f-1289">Essa classe contém os seguintes direitos estendidos para o Windows Server 2003 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2148f-1289">This class contains the following extended rights for Windows Server 2003 R2:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="2148f-1290">Nome comum</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2148f-1290">Common Name</span></span>                                                                  |
